OpenAPI Specification

IRS API

IRS API

The API of the Item Relationship Service (IRS) for retrieving item graphs along the value chain of CATENA-X partners.
More information: https://openapi-generator.tech
Contact Info: team@openapitools.org
Version: 4.5.2
BasePath:
All rights reserved
http://apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0.html

Access

  1. APIKey KeyParamName:X-API-KEY KeyInQuery:false KeyInHeader:true

AspectModels

Up 
get /irs/aspectmodels
Get all available aspect models from semantic hub or local models. (getAllAspectModels)
Get all available aspect models from semantic hub or local models.

Return type

AspectModels

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "lastUpdated" : "lastUpdated",
  "models" : [ {
    "urn" : "urn",
    "name" : "name",
    "type" : "type",
    "version" : "version",
    "status" : "status"
  }, {
    "urn" : "urn",
    "name" : "name",
    "type" : "type",
    "version" : "version",
    "status" : "status"
  } ]
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Returns all available aspect models. AspectModels

401

No valid authentication credentials. ErrorResponse

403

Authorization refused by server. ErrorResponse

EnvironmentalAndSocialStandards

Up 
get /ess/bpn/investigations/{id}
Return job with additional supplyChainImpacted information. (getBPNInvestigation)
Return job with additional supplyChainImpacted information.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — Id of the job. default: null format: uuid

Return type

Jobs

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Return job with item graph for the requested id. Jobs

400

Return job failed. ErrorResponse

401

No valid authentication credentials. ErrorResponse

403

Authorization refused by server. ErrorResponse

404

Job with the requested jobId not found. ErrorResponse
Up 
post /ess/notification/receive
Accepts notifications sent via EDC. (receiveEdcNotification)
Accepts notifications via EDC. Notifications are filtered by their type and processed accordingly.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

EdcNotificationResponseNotificationContent EdcNotificationResponseNotificationContent (required)
Body Parameter —

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Notification received successfully.

400

Notification malformed. ErrorResponse
Up 
post /ess/bpn/investigations
Registers an IRS job to start an investigation if a given bpn is contained in a part chain of a given globalAssetId. (registerBPNInvestigation)
Registers an IRS job to start an investigation if a given bpn is contained in a part chain of a given globalAssetId.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

RegisterBpnInvestigationJob RegisterBpnInvestigationJob (required)
Body Parameter —

Return type

JobHandle

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "id" : "046b6c7f-0b8a-43b9-b35d-6489e6daee91"
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

201

Returns id of registered job. JobHandle

400

Job registration failed. ErrorResponse

401

No valid authentication credentials. ErrorResponse

403

Authorization refused by server. ErrorResponse
Up 
post /irs/ess/orders
Registers an order for an ESS investigation with an array of {globalAssetIds}. Each globalAssetId will be processed in an separate job, grouped in batches. (registerESSInvestigationOrder)
Registers an order for an ESS investigation with an array of {globalAssetIds}. Each globalAssetId will be processed in an separate job, grouped in batches.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

RegisterBpnInvestigationBatchOrder RegisterBpnInvestigationBatchOrder (required)
Body Parameter —

Return type

BatchOrderCreated

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "id" : "046b6c7f-0b8a-43b9-b35d-6489e6daee91"
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.

400

401

get /irs/jobs/{id}
Return job with optional item graph result for requested id. (getJobForJobId)
Return job with optional item graph result for requested id.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — Id of the job. default: null format: uuid

Query parameters

returnUncompletedJob (optional)
Query Parameter — <true> Return job with current processed item graph. <false> Return job with item graph if job is in state COMPLETED, otherwise job. default: true

Return type

Jobs

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "relationships" : [ {
    "bpn" : "BPNL00000003AYRE",
    "catenaXId" : "urn:uuid:6c311d29-5753-46d4-b32c-19b918ea93b0",
    "aspectType" : "SingleLevelBomAsBuilt",
    "linkedItem" : {
      "hasAlternatives" : true,
      "quantity" : {
        "quantityNumber" : 1.0,
        "measurementUnit" : {
          "datatypeURI" : "urn:bamm:io.openmanufacturing:meta-model:1.0.0#piece",
          "lexicalValue" : "piece"
        }
      },

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Return job with item graph for the requested id. Jobs

206

Return job with current processed item graph for the requested id. Jobs

400

Return job failed. ErrorResponse

401

No valid authentication credentials. ErrorResponse

403

Authorization refused by server. ErrorResponse

404

Job with the requested jobId not found. ErrorResponse
Up 
get /irs/jobs
Returns paginated jobs with state and execution times. (getJobsByJobStates)
Returns paginated jobs with state and execution times.

Query parameters

states (optional)
Query Parameter — Requested job states. default: null
page (optional)
Query Parameter — Zero-based page index (0..N) default: 0
size (optional)
Query Parameter — The size of the page to be returned default: 20
sort (optional)
Query Parameter — Sorting criteria in the format: property,(asc|desc). Default sort order is ascending. Multiple sort criteria are supported. default: null

Return type

PageResult

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "pageCount" : 0,
  "pageNumber" : 6,
  "pageSize" : 1,
  "content" : [ {
    "completedOn" : "2000-01-23T04:56:07.000+00:00",
    "id" : "046b6c7f-0b8a-43b9-b35d-6489e6daee91",
    "state" : "UNSAVED",
    "startedOn" : "2000-01-23T04:56:07.000+00:00"
  }, {
    "completedOn" : "2000-01-23T04:56:07.000+00:00",
    "id" : "046b6c7f-0b8a-43b9-b35d-6489e6daee91",
    "state" : "UNSAVED",
    "startedOn" : "2000-01-23T04:56:07.000+00:00"
  } ],
  "totalElements" : 5
}

String Callback url to notify requestor when job processing is finished. There are four uri variable placeholders that can be used: orderId, batchId, orderState and batchState.

Boolean Flag to specify whether aspects should be requested and collected. Default is false.
